  `feature` varchar(255)  NOT NULL,
  `user` varchar(255)  NOT NULL,
  `permissioncode` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`feature`,`user`),
  KEY `FK974CAFDA61C18596` (`feature`),
  KEY `FK974CAFDAE8E8F059` (`user`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK974CAFDAE8E8F059` FOREIGN KEY (`user`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK974CAFDA61C18596` FOREIGN KEY (`feature`) REFERENCES `featurelist` (`featureid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `role` (
  `id` varchar(255)  NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(50)  NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `name` (`name`),
  KEY `FK3580767E350557` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK3580767E350557` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

INSERT INTO `role` (id,name,company) VALUES ('1', 'Company Administrator', null),
('2', 'Company User', null),
('ff80808122787f070122787f13620002', 'Super Administrator', 'ff80808122787f070122787f13560001');

alter table `users` ADD COLUMN `role` varchar(255) default NULL;
update `users` set role='1' where roleid=1;
update `users` set role='2' where roleid=0;
update `users` set role='ff80808122787f070122787f13620002' where userid='ff80808122787f070122787f13620002';
alter table `users` DROP COLUMN `roleid`;

alter table `users` ADD FOREIGN KEY (`role`) REFERENCES `role` (`id`);

drop table if exists userpermission;

CREATE TABLE `userpermission` (
  `feature` varchar(255)  NOT NULL,
  `role` varchar(255)  NOT NULL,
  `permissioncode` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`feature`,`role`),
  KEY `FK974CAFDAE8E619AF` (`role`),
  KEY `FK974CAFDA61C18596` (`feature`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK974CAFDA61C18596` FOREIGN KEY (`feature`) REFERENCES `featurelist` (`featureid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK974CAFDAE8E619AF` FOREIGN KEY (`role`) REFERENCES `role` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `purchaseorder` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `ponumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `shipto` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `shipvia` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `deliverydate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  KEY `FKB1F87AED4FCB79C5` (`journalentry`),
  KEY `FKB1F87AED7E350557` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKB1F87AED4FCB79C5` FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKB1F87AED7E350557` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `podetails` (
  `po` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `inventory` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`po`,`inventory`),
  KEY `FK456BF7638A800BFD` (`po`),
  KEY `FK456BF7639BBDE669` (`inventory`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK456BF7638A800BFD` FOREIGN KEY (`po`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK456BF7639BBDE669` FOREIGN KEY (`inventory`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `debitnote` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `dnnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `memo` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `discount` double NOT NULL,
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `purchaseOrder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  KEY `FKE077EEDE3C7878EB` (`purchaseOrder`),
  KEY `FKE077EEDE4FCB79C5` (`journalentry`),
  KEY `FKE077EEDE7E350557` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKE077EEDE3C7878EB` FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseOrder`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKE077EEDE4FCB79C5` FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKE077EEDE7E350557` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `dndetails` (
  `debitnote` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `inventory` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`debitnote`,`inventory`),
  KEY `FKEA5596784D7F058D` (`debitnote`),
  KEY `FKEA5596789BBDE669` (`inventory`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKEA5596784D7F058D` FOREIGN KEY (`debitnote`) REFERENCES `debitnote` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKEA5596789BBDE669` FOREIGN KEY (`inventory`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `payment` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `paymentnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `paymentMethod` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `paymentdetail` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `purchaseOrder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  UNIQUE KEY `paymentdetail` (`paymentdetail`),
  KEY `FKD11C32063C7878EB` (`purchaseOrder`),
  KEY `FKD11C3206A5632C1F` (`paymentMethod`),
  KEY `FKD11C32064FCB79C5` (`journalentry`),
  KEY `FKD11C32067E350557` (`company`),
  KEY `FKD11C320686ABBAFF` (`paymentdetail`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKD11C32063C7878EB` FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseOrder`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKD11C32064FCB79C5` FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKD11C32067E350557` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKD11C320686ABBAFF` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentdetail`) REFERENCES `paymentdetail` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKD11C3206A5632C1F` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentMethod`) REFERENCES `paymentmethod` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

CREATE TABLE `defaultaccount` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `openingbalance` double NOT NULL,
  `groupname` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `parent` varchar(255) default NULL,

  FOREIGN KEY (`groupname`) REFERENCES `accgroup` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

ALTER TABLE `customer` DROP FOREIGN KEY `FK24217FDE9E1502CA`;
ALTER TABLE `customer` MODIFY COLUMN `preferedDeliveryMode` int(11) NOT NULL default '1';
ALTER TABLE `vendor` DROP FOREIGN KEY `FKCF1EA5489E1502CA`;
ALTER TABLE `vendor` MODIFY COLUMN `preferedDeliveryMode` int(11) NOT NULL default '1';
ALTER TABLE `receipt` DROP FOREIGN KEY `FK4082723886ABBAFF`;
ALTER TABLE `receipt` DROP FOREIGN KEY `FK40827238A5632C1F`;
ALTER TABLE `receipt` DROP COLUMN `paymentdetail`;
ALTER TABLE `receipt` DROP COLUMN `paymentMethod`;
DROP TABLE `cndiscount`;
DROP TABLE `cndetails`;
DROP TABLE `creditnote`;
DROP TABLE `masteritem`;
DROP TABLE `paymentdetail`;

ALTER TABLE `invoice` DROP COLUMN `shipvia`;

CREATE TABLE `card` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `cardno` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `cardholder` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `address` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `expirydate` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `zipcode` varchar(6) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `cheque` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `chequeno` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `bankname` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `description` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `paydetail` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `paymentMethod` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `card` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `cheque` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`card`) REFERENCES `card` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`cheque`) REFERENCES `cheque` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


ALTER TABLE `receipt` ADD COLUMN `paydetail` varchar(255) default NULL, ADD  FOREIGN KEY (`paydetail`) REFERENCES `paydetail` (`id`);

CREATE TABLE `creditnote` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `seq` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `cnnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `memo` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `cndetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `inventory` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `invoiceRow` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `creditNote` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `discount` (`discount`),
  UNIQUE KEY `inventory` (`inventory`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`invoiceRow`) REFERENCES `invoicedetails` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`inventory`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`creditNote`) REFERENCES `creditnote` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `cndiscount` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `invoice` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `creditnote` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `discount` (`discount`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`invoice`) REFERENCES `invoice` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`creditnote`) REFERENCES `creditnote` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `masteritem` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `value` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `masterGroup` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`masterGroup`) REFERENCES `mastergroup` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `goodsreceipt` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `grnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `billfrom` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `shipfrom` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `shipdate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `duedate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `centry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `sentry` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `oentry` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `centry` (`centry`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  UNIQUE KEY `discount` (`discount`),
  UNIQUE KEY `sentry` (`sentry`),
  UNIQUE KEY `oentry` (`oentry`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`centry`) REFERENCES `jedetail` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`oentry`) REFERENCES `jedetail` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`sentry`) REFERENCES `jedetail` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `grdetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `rate` double NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `goodsreceipt` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `discount` (`discount`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`id`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`goodsreceipt`) REFERENCES `goodsreceipt` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE `debitnote` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `seq` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `dnnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `memo` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `dndetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `inventory` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `goodsReceiptRow` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `debitNote` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `discount` (`discount`),
  UNIQUE KEY `inventory` (`inventory`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`debitNote`) REFERENCES `debitnote` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`goodsReceiptRow`) REFERENCES `grdetails` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`inventory`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `dndiscount` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `goodsreceipt` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `debitnote` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `discount` (`discount`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`debitnote`) REFERENCES `debitnote` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`goodsreceipt`) REFERENCES `goodsreceipt` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `payment` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `paymentnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `journalentry` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `paydetail` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `journalentry` (`journalentry`),
  UNIQUE KEY `paydetail` (`paydetail`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`paydetail`) REFERENCES `paydetail` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `paymentdetail` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `paymentid` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `paymentthrough` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `description` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `amount` double default NULL,
  `payment` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `goodsReceipt` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`payment`) REFERENCES `payment` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`goodsReceipt`) REFERENCES `goodsreceipt` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `purchaseorder` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `ponumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `orderdate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `duedate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `vendor` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`vendor`) REFERENCES `vendor` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `podetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `remark` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rate` double NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `purchaseorder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseorder`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `salesorder` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `sonumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `orderdate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `duedate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `customer` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`customer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `sodetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `remark` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rate` double NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `salesorder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`salesorder`) REFERENCES `salesorder` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  KEY `FK82087052AF1ECEC2` (`taxentry`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK82087052AF1ECEC2` FOREIGN KEY (`taxentry`) REFERENCES `jedetail` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK820870524FCB79C5` FOREIGN KEY (`journalentry`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK820870526E04410A` FOREIGN KEY (`centry`) REFERENCES `jedetail` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK820870526EBB7297` FOREIGN KEY (`crntry`) REFERENCES `jedetail` (`id`),

CREATE TABLE `uploadedfiles` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `filename` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `filepathname` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `tablename` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `importon` timestamp NOT NULL default CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `company` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `company` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `uploadedfiles_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

update defaultgst set description='Goods And Services Tax(BL) - Purchases with GST incurred but not claimable under Regulations 26/27 (e.g. medical expenses for staff)' where name='GST(BL)@7.00%';
update defaultgst set description='Goods And Services Tax(NR) - Purchase from non GST-registered supplier with no GST incurred' where name='GST(NR)@0.00%';
update defaultgst set description='Goods And Services Tax(ZP) - Purchase from GST-registered supplier with no GST incurred. (e.g. supplier provides transportation of goods that qualify as international services)' where name='GST(ZP)@0.00%';
update defaultgst set description='Goods And Services Tax(EP) - Purchases exempted from GST. E.g. purchase of residential property or financial services' where name='GST(EP)@0.00%';

CREATE TABLE `deliveryorder` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `donumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `orderdate` datetime NOT NULL,  
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `customer` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,  
  `costcenter` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `status` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FK_COMPANY` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_CUSTOMER` (`customer`),  
  KEY `FK_COSTCENTER` (`costcenter`),
  KEY `FK_STATUS` (`status`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_STATUS` FOREIGN KEY (`status`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_COSTCENTER` FOREIGN KEY (`costcenter`) REFERENCES `costcenter` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_COMPANY` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_CUSTOMER` FOREIGN KEY (`customer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE `dodetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `remark` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `actualquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
 `deliveredquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `deliveryorder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) default '0',
  `description` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `sodetails` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `cidetails` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FKCOMPANY` (`company`),
  KEY `FKID` (`id`),
  KEY `FKPRODUCT` (`product`),
  KEY `FKDELIVERYORDER` (`deliveryorder`),
  KEY `FKSODETAILS` (`sodetails`),
  KEY `FKCIDETAILS` (`cidetails`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKID` FOREIGN KEY (`id`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKCOMPANY` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKPRODUCT` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKDELIVERYORDER` FOREIGN KEY (`deliveryorder`) REFERENCES `deliveryorder` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKSODETAILS` FOREIGN KEY (`sodetails`) REFERENCES `sodetails` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKCIDETAILS` FOREIGN KEY (`cidetails`) REFERENCES `invoicedetails` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
  `docid` varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
  `docname` varchar(255)  NOT NULL ,
  `doctypeid` varchar(255) NULL default '',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `invoicedoccompmap` ( 
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL ,	
  `documentid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `invoiceid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FKDOCUMENT` (`documentid`),  
  KEY `FKCOMP` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKCOMP` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKDOCUMENT` FOREIGN KEY (`documentid`) REFERENCES `invoicedocuments` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `grorder` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `gronumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `grorderdate` datetime NOT NULL,  
  `memo` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `vendor` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,  
  `costcenter` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `status` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FK_GRCOMPANY` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_GRVENDOR` (`vendor`),  
  KEY `FK_GRCOSTCENTER` (`costcenter`),
  KEY `FK_GRSTATUS` (`status`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_GRSTATUS` FOREIGN KEY (`status`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_GRCOSTCENTER` FOREIGN KEY (`costcenter`) REFERENCES `costcenter` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_GRCOMPANY` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_GRVENDOR` FOREIGN KEY (`vendor`) REFERENCES `vendor` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `grodetails` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `remark` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `actualquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `deliveredquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `grorder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) default '0',
  `description` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `videtails` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FKGRDCOMPANY` (`company`),
  KEY `FKGRDID` (`id`),
  KEY `FKGRDPRODUCT` (`product`),
  KEY `FKGRDGRORDER` (`grorder`),
  KEY `FKGRDVIDETAILS` (`videtails`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKGRDID` FOREIGN KEY (`id`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKGRDCOMPANY` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKGRDPRODUCT` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKGRDGRORDER` FOREIGN KEY (`grorder`) REFERENCES `grorder` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKGRDCIDETAILS` FOREIGN KEY (`videtails`) REFERENCES `grdetails` (`id`)
)ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

/*Billing Customer invoices*/
alter table billinginvoicedetails add column crntryflag int(2) default 0;
select count(*) from billinginvoice where crntry not in (select id from jedetail);
update billinginvoicedetails inner join billinginvoice on billinginvoice.id = billinginvoicedetails.billinginvoice set billinginvoicedetails.crntry = billinginvoice.crntry , crntryflag = 1 where billinginvoice.crntry is not null;

/*Billing Sales order*/
alter table billingsodetails add column crntryflag int(2) default 0;
update billingsodetails inner join billingsalesorder on billingsalesorder.id = billingsodetails.salesorder set billingsodetails.creditto = billingsalesorder.creditto , crntryflag = 1 where billingsalesorder.creditto is not null;

/*Billing Vendor invoices*/
alter table billinggrdetails add column crntryflag int(2) default 0;
select count(*) from billinggr where crntry not in (select id from jedetail);
update billinggrdetails inner join billinggr on billinggr.id = billinggrdetails.billinggreceipt set billinggrdetails.crntry = billinggr.crntry , crntryflag = 1 where billinggr.crntry is not null;

/*Billing Purchase order*/
alter table billingpodetails add column crntryflag int(2) default 0;
update billingpodetails inner join billingpurchaseorder on billingpurchaseorder.id = billingpodetails.purchaseorder set billingpodetails.debitfrom = billingpurchaseorder.debitfrom , crntryflag = 1 where billingpurchaseorder.debitfrom is not null;

alter table billinginvoice drop  foreign key`FK820870526EBB7297`;
alter table billingsalesorder drop foreign key `FK9628A7DD9A35552`;
alter table billinggr drop  foreign key `FK6CF57CA66EBB7297`;
alter table billingpurchaseorder drop foreign key  `FKAF5B78524D70CCB4`;

alter TABLE  billinginvoice drop column `crntry` ;
alter TABLE  billinggr drop column `crntry`;
alter TABLE  billingsalesorder drop column  `creditto` ;
alter TABLE  billingpurchaseorder drop column  `debitfrom`;

alter TABLE  billinginvoicedetails drop column  `crntryflag`;
alter table billingsodetails drop column crntryflag;
alter table billinggrdetails drop column crntryflag;
alter table billingpodetails drop column crntryflag;

CREATE TABLE `accountbudget` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,  
  `account` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `jan` double default -1,
  `feb` double default -1,
  `march` double default -1,
  `april` double default -1,
  `may` double default -1,
  `june` double default -1,
  `july` double default -1,
  `aug` double default -1,
  `sept` double default -1,
  `oct` double default -1,
  `nov` double default -1,
  `dec` double default -1,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),  
  KEY `FK_accountbudget_acc` (`account`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_accountbudget_acc` FOREIGN KEY (`account`) REFERENCES `account` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `purchaserequisition` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `prnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `requisitiondate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `duedate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(1024) DEFAULT '',
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `tax` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `vendor` varchar(40) default '',
  `company` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `users` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `discount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `perdiscount` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `archieve` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `approvestatuslevel` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `currency` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `templateid` varchar(40) DEFAULT 'ff80808140a555fe0140a588bcee0007',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`tax`) REFERENCES `tax` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`users`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`currency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE `purchaserequisitiondetail` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `remark` varchar(255) DEFAULT '',
  `approverremark` varchar(1024) DEFAULT '',
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rate` double NOT NULL,
  `tax` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `product` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `purchaserequisition` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `discount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `discountispercent` int(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`tax`) REFERENCES `tax` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT  FOREIGN KEY (`purchaserequisition`) REFERENCES `purchaserequisition` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',

CREATE TABLE salesreturn (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `srnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `orderdate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(1024) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `customer` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `costcenter` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `shipvia` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `fob` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `shipdate` datetime default NULL,
  `templateid` varchar(255) default 'ff80808140a555fe0140a588bcee0007',
    `favouriteflag` int(1) default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_COMPANY_salesreturn` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_COSTCENTER_salesreturn` FOREIGN KEY (`costcenter`) REFERENCES `costcenter` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_CUSTOMER_salesreturn` FOREIGN KEY (`customer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

CREATE TABLE srdetails (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `remark` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `actualquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `returnquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `salesreturn` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) default '0',
  `description` varchar(1024) default NULL,
  `dodetails` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `partno` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKCOMPANY_srdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKSALESRETURN_srdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`salesreturn`) REFERENCES `salesreturn` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKID_srdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`id`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKPRODUCT_srdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKDODETAILS_srdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`dodetails`) REFERENCES `dodetails` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

CREATE TABLE `layoutgroup` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `nature` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sequence` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `template` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `parent` varchar(255) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FK802BA69E7E350557_layoutgroup` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK802BA69E7E350557_layoutgroup` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  KEY `template_layoutgroup` (`template`),
  CONSTRAINT `template_layoutgroup` FOREIGN KEY (`template`) REFERENCES `templatepnl` (`id`),
  KEY `parent_layoutgroup` (`parent`),
  CONSTRAINT `parent_layoutgroup` FOREIGN KEY (`parent`) REFERENCES `layoutgroup` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `defaultHeader` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `moduleName` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `flag` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `configid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pojoheadername` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `recordname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `xtype` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pojomethodname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `validatetype` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `maxlength` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `ismandatory` char(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `required` char(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `hbmnotnull` char(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `defaultvalue` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `refmodule_pojoclassname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `refdatacolumn_hbmname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reffetchcolumn_hbmname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `allowimport` char(1) DEFAULT '1',
  `customflag` char(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `allowmapping` char(1) DEFAULT 'T',
  `dbcolumnname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reftablename` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reftablefk` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reftabledatacolumn` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dummyvalue` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `module` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK6CE0AE4B165B5A50` (`module`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE `customdesigntemplate` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `templatename` varchar(100) DEFAULT '',
  `moduleid` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `html` text,
  `json` text,
  `sqlquery` varchar(4000) DEFAULT NULL,
  `isdefault` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdon` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `createdby` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `company` (`company`),
  CONSTRAINT `customdesigntemplate_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

//Sagar - 14th Nov, 2013, CN for paid invoices

alter table creditnote add column `cntype`  int(1) default 1;
alter table cndetails add column `paidinvflag` int(1) default 0;

alter table debitnote add column `dntype`  int(1) default 1;
alter table dndetails add column `paidinvflag` int(1) default 0;

//Malhari Post text for Invoices 15 Nov
ALTER TABLE `invoice`
ADD COLUMN `posttext`  longtext NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `istemplate`;

ALTER TABLE `billinginvoice`
ADD COLUMN `posttext`  longtext NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `istemplate`;

ALTER TABLE `goodsreceipt`
ADD COLUMN `posttext`  longtext NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `istemplate`;

ALTER TABLE `billinggr`
ADD COLUMN `posttext`  longtext NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `istemplate`;

//Sagar A - 15th Nov, 2013, updated old records
ALTER TABLE `compaccpreferences`
ADD COLUMN `negativestock`  int(3) NULL DEFAULT 1 AFTER `pdfposttext`,
ADD COLUMN `custcreditcontrol`  int(3) NULL DEFAULT 2 AFTER `negativestock`;

update creditnote set otherwise = 'F'  where  otherwise in ('0');
update debitnote set otherwise = 'F'  where  otherwise in ('0');

update creditnote inner join journalentry on journalentry.id = creditnote.journalentry inner join jedetail on jedetail.journalEntry = journalentry.id 
set cnamount = jedetail.amount, customer = jedetail.account, cntype = 2 where jedetail.debit = 'F' and creditnote.otherwise = 'T';

update debitnote inner join journalentry on journalentry.id = debitnote.journalentry inner join jedetail on jedetail.journalEntry = journalentry.id
 set dnamount = jedetail.amount, vendor = jedetail.account, dntype = 2 where jedetail.debit = 'T' and debitnote.otherwise = 'T';

// Sagar M - 18-11-2013. 1. Accept payment from Vendor 2. Make payment to customer

alter table `receipt` ADD COLUMN `vendor` varchar(40) default NULL;
alter table `receipt` ADD COLUMN `receipttype` int default 0;

alter table `payment` ADD COLUMN `customer` varchar(40) default NULL;
alter table `payment` ADD COLUMN `receipttype` int default 0;

//Sagar A - 18th Nov, 2013,     CN/DN against vendor and customer resp
alter table creditnote add column `vendor` varchar(255) default NULL;
alter table debitnote add column `customer` varchar(255) default NULL;

//Malhari - 18th Nov 2013. Purchase Return flow
CREATE TABLE purchasereturn (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `prnumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `orderdate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `memo` varchar(1024) default NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,
  `vendor` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `costcenter` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `shipvia` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `fob` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `shipdate` datetime default NULL,
  `templateid` varchar(255) default 'ff80808140a555fe0140a588bcee0007',
   `favouriteflag` int(1) default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_COMPANY_purchasereturn` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_COSTCENTER_purchasereturn` FOREIGN KEY (`costcenter`) REFERENCES `costcenter` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_VENDOR_purchasereturn` FOREIGN KEY (`vendor`) REFERENCES `vendor` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

CREATE TABLE prdetails (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `remark` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `actualquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `returnquantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `purchasereturn` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `srno` int(11) default '0',
  `description` varchar(1024) default NULL,
  `grdetails` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `partno` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKCOMPANY_prdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKPURCHASERETURN_prdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`purchasereturn`) REFERENCES `purchasereturn` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKID_prdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`id`) REFERENCES `inventory` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKPRODUCT_prdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FKDODETAILS_prdetails` FOREIGN KEY (`grdetails`) REFERENCES `grodetails` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

alter table compaccpreferences add prnoformat varchar(50) default NULL;

// Sagar M - Invoice Terms 23th Nov 2013


CREATE TABLE `invoicetermssales` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `formula` varchar(1024) DEFAULT NULL,
  `category` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sign` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `includegst` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `includeprofit` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `supressamount` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `account` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE `invoicetermsmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `invoice` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `term` (`term`),
  KEY `invoice` (`invoice`),
  CONSTRAINT `invoicetermsmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `invoicetermsmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`invoice`) REFERENCES `invoice` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

//Sagar M -Sales Terms 22 Nov 2013
CREATE TABLE `receipttermsmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `goodsreceipt` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `term` (`term`),
  KEY `goodsreceipt` (`goodsreceipt`),
  CONSTRAINT `receipttermsmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `receipttermsmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`goodsreceipt`) REFERENCES `goodsreceipt` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

//Malhari Pawar 01/12/2013 Added changes for Payment against CN and DN
CREATE TABLE `creditnotpayment` (
`id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`cnid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`paymentid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`amountdue`  double NULL ,
`amountpaid`  double NULL ,
 PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_CreditNoteid` FOREIGN KEY (`cnid`) REFERENCES `creditnote` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
CONSTRAINT `FK_paymentid` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentid`) REFERENCES `payment` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE `debitnotepayment` (
`id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`dnid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`receiptid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`amountdue`  double NULL ,
`amountpaid`  double NULL ,
 PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_DebititNoteid` FOREIGN KEY (`dnid`) REFERENCES `debitnote` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
CONSTRAINT `FK_receiptid` FOREIGN KEY (`receiptid`) REFERENCES `receipt` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
);

CREATE TABLE `receivecreditnotepayment` (
`id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`cnid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`receiptid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`amountdue`  double NULL ,
`amountpaid`  double NULL ,
 PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_receivecreditnotepayment` FOREIGN KEY (`cnid`) REFERENCES `creditnote` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
CONSTRAINT `FK_receivereceiptid` FOREIGN KEY (`receiptid`) REFERENCES `receipt` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
);
CREATE TABLE `makedebitnotepayment` (
`id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`dnid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`paymentid`  varchar(255) NULL ,
`amountdue`  double NULL ,
`amountpaid`  double NULL ,
 PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
CONSTRAINT `FK_makedebitnotepayment` FOREIGN KEY (`dnid`) REFERENCES `debitnote` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
CONSTRAINT `FK_receiptiddebitnote` FOREIGN KEY (`paymentid`) REFERENCES `receipt` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
);

  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `applydate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `price` double NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(255) NOT NULL,

  `affecteduser` varchar(255) default NULL,

  CONSTRAINT `STOCK_FK815695677E350557` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `STOCK_FK815695678E4485CF` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

update product set purchaseuom=unitOfMeasure,salesuom=unitOfMeasure,purchasetostockuomvalue=1,salestostockuomvalue=1;
update inventory set convertedquantity=actquantity;

CREATE TABLE `vendorquotationtermmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `vendorquotation` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `vendorquotationtermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `vendorquotationtermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`vendorquotation`) REFERENCES `vendorquotation` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `purchaseorder` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` tinyint(3) unsigned DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseordertermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseordertermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseorder`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `salesorder` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,

  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,

  CONSTRAINT `salesordertermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`salesorder`) REFERENCES `salesorder` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
